about independence, frustration, and not liking to be told what to do. The biggest thing that helps is taking the
pressure way down. The more we push,...

  _Full excerpt:_ Night time potty training isn’t a thing. Kids naturally will hold their bladder overnight with time. A lot of it has to do with
hormones as they mature. It is not advisable to wake them; you’ll disrupt their circadian rhythm, which is crucial for
this part of their development.

  _Full excerpt:_ Right now, the potty feels like a game to him and that’s okay. I wouldn’t stop him sitting or exploring. But I would
gently shift it from “play station” to “quick potty stop.”
Here’s what helped me:
• Keep potty sits short (2–3 minutes max). If nothing happens, say calmly: “All done. We’ll try again later.”
• Offer the potty at predictable times like after waking, after meals, before bath.
• If he...

developmental. The screaming around the potty usually means he’s overwhelmed, not refusing. It...

---


## Key Insights

1. **Exhaustion** is the dominant emotional dimension in Layer 5 Kommentare, appearing in 518 of 1741 total comments (29.8%).

1. The fear dimension captures parental anxiety about potty training regression, medical concerns, and fear of 'never getting it right' (439 comments, 25.2%).

1. Guilt manifests as parents blaming themselves for not training earlier, not being consistent, or feeling like they've failed their child (177 comments, 10.2%).

1. Exhaustion reflects the burnout of repeated accidents, cleaning up, and the emotional toll of the process (518 comments, 29.8%).

1. Fear and exhaustion overlap significantly (161 comments) — these emotions compound in parents dealing with prolonged potty training struggles.
